# ::id PROXY_AFP_ENG_20020117_0270.17 ::date 2013-05-09T11:11:34 ::snt-type body ::annotator LDC-AMR-14 ::preferred
# ::snt The ban was strictly enforced with opium production decreasing from 3,200 tons to 185 tons.
# ::save-date Wed Dec 11, 2013 ::file PROXY_AFP_ENG_20020117_0270_17.txt
(e / enforce-01
      :ARG1 (b / ban-01)
      :manner (s / strict)
      :ARG0-of (c / cause-01
            :ARG1 (d / decrease-01
                  :ARG1 (p / produce-01
                        :ARG1 (o / opium))
                  :ARG3 (m / mass-quantity :quant 3200
                        :unit (t / ton))
                  :ARG4 (m2 / mass-quantity :quant 185
                        :unit (t2 / ton)))))

# ::id PROXY_AFP_ENG_20020123_0334.6 ::date 2013-05-18T14:05:25 ::snt-type body ::annotator LDC-AMR-14 ::preferred

                  :ARG0 f

                        :quant (m / more-than :op1 1600)))

                  :location (a4 / and

                              :part-of c)
                        :op2 (s2 / south
                              :part-of c))

                        :op1 (n4 / now)
